Challenge 20: May the Force be with you

A long time ago in a galaxy far, far away....

The small, spartan hovel is cluttered with desert junk but still manages to radiate an air of time-worn comfort and security. Luke is in one corner repairing Threepio's arm, as old Ben sits thinking.

LUKE: No, my father didn't fight in the wars. He was a navigator on a spice freighter.

BEN: That's what your uncle told you. He didn't hold with your father's ideals. Thought he should have stayed here and not gotten involved.

LUKE: You fought in the Clone Wars?

BEN: Yes, I was once a Jedi Knight the same as your father.

LUKE: I wish I'd known him.

BEN: He was the best star-pilot in the galaxy, and a cunning warrior. I understand you've become quite a good pilot yourself. And he was a good friend. Which reminds me...

Ben gets up and goes to a chest where he rummages around. As Luke finishes repairing Threepio and starts to fit the restraining bolt back on, Threepio looks at him nervously. Luke thinks about the bolt for a moment then puts it on the table. Ben shuffles up and presents Luke with a short handle with several electronic gadgets attached to it.

BEN: I have something here for you. Your father wanted you to have this when you were old enough, but your uncle wouldn't allow it. He feared you might follow old Obi-Wan on some damned-fool idealistic crusade like your father did.

THREEPIO: Sir, if you'll not be needing me, I'll close down for a while.

LUKE: Sure, go ahead.

Ben hands Luke the saber.

LUKE: What is it?

BEN: Your father's lightsaber. This is the weapon of a Jedi Knight. Not as clumsy or as random as a blaster.

Luke pushes a button on the handle. A long beam shoots out about four feet and flickers there. The light plays across the ceiling.

BEN: An elegant weapon for a more civilized time. For over a thousand generations the Jedi Knights were the guardians of peace and justice in the Old Republic. Before the dark times, before the Empire.

Luke hasn't really been listening.

LUKE: How did my father die?

BEN: A young Jedi named Darth Vader, who was a pupil of mine until he turned to evil, helped the Empire hunt down and destroy the Jedi Knights. He betrayed and murdered your father. Now the Jedi are all but extinct. Vader was seduced by the dark side of the Force.

LUKE: The Force?

BEN: Well, the Force is what gives a Jedi his power. It's an energy field created by all living things. It surrounds us and penetrates us. It binds the galaxy together.

Artoo makes beeping sounds.

BEN: Now, let's see if we can't figure out what you are, my little friend. And where you come from.

LUKE: I saw part of the message he was...

Luke is cut short as the recorded image of the beautiful young Rebel princess is projected from Artoo's face.

BEN: I seem to have found it.

Luke stops his work as the lovely girl's image flickers before his eyes.

LEIA: General Kenobi, years ago you served my father in the Clone Wars. Now he begs you to help him in his struggle against the Empire. I regret that I am unable to present my father's request to you in person, but my ship has fallen under attack and I'm afraid my mission to bring you to Alderaan has failed. I have placed information vital to the survival of the Rebellion into the memory systems of this R2 unit. My father will know how to retrieve it. You must see this droid safely delivered to him on Alderaan. This is our most desperate hour. Help me, Obi-Wan Kenobi, you're my only hope.

There is a little static and the transmission is cut short. Old Ben leans back and scratches his head. He silently puffs on a tarnished chrome water pipe. Luke has stars in his eyes.

BEN: You must learn the ways of the Force if you're to come with me to Alderaan.

May the Force be with you

Artoo is entrusted with a message from Princess Leia that he is to deliver to Obi-Wan Kenobi, and it is imperative that the message not be intercepted by the Empire; that is why Artoo set up an elaborate encryption system around Princess Leia's stream. If you take a closer look at the video you will notice that, as soon as Obi-Wan Kenobi taps Artoo, the full stream is played. A not-that-known fact is that, having touched the droid, Obi-wan played a key game with Artoo through the power of the Force, which resulted in them exchanging a key used in Alderaan encryption strategy. Streaming the key with the Force, Obi-Wan is decrypting Leia's stream on the fly, as seen in the video. Another not-so-known fact is that, along with Leia's stream, Artoo is also streaming a special message - a key that Obi-Wan will need to disable the tractor beam on board the Death Star.

Your task is to find this key.

The mentioned Force-powered key game that Artoo and Obi-Wan play to agree on an Alderaan encryption strategy key is defined as follows:

  • Obi-Wan creates 1000 messages of format "Key=<actual key> & Puzzle=<game index>"
  • Obi-Wan encrypts these messages using an old system he learned from Yoda in Dagobah System called Dagobah encryption strategy, intentionally using a weak key (only 4 most significant bytes of entropy).
  • Obi-Wan sends these encrypted messages to Artoo.
  • Artoo chooses one of the games at random, using his Droid boost library's implementation of pseudo-random number generators (as defined in <droids/boost/random/twister.hpp>)
  • Artoo magically decrypts that randomly chosen message and inside finds
    "Key=<Artoo's actual key> & Puzzle=<Artoo's game index>"
  • Artoo now sends Obi-Wan, via the Local Force Network interface, a message containing Artoo's game index.
  • Key used is now known to both Artoo and Obi-Wan: the Artoo's actual key.
You, as a Sith Apprentice, face a challenging task of recovering the key for disabling the tractor beam on board the Death Star, by sensing the disturbance in the Force during the transfers.

Images from Star Wars Motion Picture Â© Lucasfilm Ltd all rights reserved

Input

The input contains multiple entries of the format: <encrypted message>:<1000 encrypted game messages, hex encoded, delimited with ~ character>

Output

One line for each intput entry.

Sample input

(5 entries follow): Submit & test your code

To test and submit code we provide a set of tools to help you. Download contest tools if you haven't already done that. You will then be able to test and submit your solution to this challenge with the challenge token.

Challenge token: UTHjxUUg7sIi5bWfTLwS

To test your program

./test_challenge UTHjxUUg7sIi5bWfTLwS path/program

A nice output will tell you if your program got the right solution or not. You can try as many times as you need.

To submit your program to the challenge

./submit_challenge UTHjxUUg7sIi5bWfTLwS path/source_pkg.tgz path/program

Note that you first need to solve the test phase before submitting the code. During the submit phase we might give your program harder questions, so try to make your program failsafe.

Remember you can only submit once! Once your solution is submitted you won't be able to amend it to fix issues or make it faster, so please be sure your program is finished before submitting it.

If you have any doubts, please check the help section.

Go ahead

I'm done! :)

Once you have submitted your code, hit refresh and continue to next challenge.

I'm stuck! :(

Be sure you follow the Tuenti Engineering twitter for updates and possible hints during the contest.

If this challenge is too hard and you are blocked, you will be able to skip it after two hours. Note that you won't be able to complete it later, and you have a limited number of challenges to skip.

Finally, if you run out of skips but are still really stuck with one problem, you will be able to skip it after 24 hours.
